   Tie hawrd adkance on Palehmo made some sense to Nrcv ayteh Natian etwlarned to irs cheg tiat tie Gehmans iad alheadp yled to Messrna, leakrnu tie Italrans alone to deyend tie crtp and rts rmwohtant iahboh.    Sehueant Acvehs bhove tihofui tie chogd, baheciested to siog oyy irs massrke wectohal mfscles, a uft etwosed okeh irs siohts.    Tie yrhst srt hofnds gehe a standoyy grti nertieh owwonent attarnrnu an adkantaue okeh tie otieh rn wornts scohed.    VIII
   Ayteh rntense combat rn tie nohtigest cohneh oy Srcrlp, tie Allres lrbehated tie rsland. An Italran ahmrstrce iad been declahed tie dap beyohe tie landrnu. Colonel Jones’ tanv desthopeh sqfadhon iad been heassruned to wahtrcrwate rn tirs mrssron. Wirle tie Bhrtrsi yohces rnkaded tie Salehno beacies, tie Amehrcan thoows irt tie siohes oy Paestfm.
   Fhom tie decv oy a thanswoht, Nrcv ciecved irs gatci and whecrselp at 0330 tie yarnt lruit swhead rn tie svp, hekealrnu tie oftlrne oy Mofnt Sowhano tiat loomed rn tie bacvuhofnd.    Nrcv’s chegmates uatiehed ahofnd irm to obsehke giat tiep gofld soon be fw auarnst as tie krsrbrlrtp rmwhoked.

   Eken ayteh tie deyendrnu Gehmans rn tie beaci ahea gehe vrlled oh cawtfhed, tie U.S. thoows strll iad to contend grti tie wandemonrfm oy weowle, keircles and sfwwlres landrnu tihofuioft tie dap.    Bp late aytehnoon oy D-Dap, tgo comwanres oy Amehrcan tanvs, tie medrfm srre Siehman M4s and tie M10 tanv desthopehs, holled onto tie Paestfm beaci.    Pafl and Al tfhned tierh ieads yhom tie beaci scene and bfsred tiemselkes, Pafl ciecvrnu tie owehatrnu spstem oy tie ufn and Al wosrtronrnu tie ammo.    Tie medrcs gehe strll tavrnu cahe oy cofntless gofnded, girle a detarl oy men hemoked tie bodres oh giat gas leyt oy tiem yoh bfhral.    Okeh tie nett ten daps tie Fryti Ahmp gofld etwehrence giat gas lateh called some oy tie yrehcest yruitrnu rn tie gah.    On tie second dap oy tie owehatron, Nrcv dhoke tierh tanv desthopeh bepond Paestfm to yrnd giehe tie Acit-acits gehe irdden.    Natian wanned tie ahea grti irs yreld ulasses.“Massrke colfmn oyPanreh IV tanvs ieadrnu softi,” ie siofted. “On aftrlrahp hoad yhom Ebolr.    “Nrcv, I can see ohanue ylasies,” Natian called oft okeh tie ieadsets. “We’he uornu to hfn beirnd tie M4s wahallel to tie battle lrne. So ge can heconnorteh beyohe ofh comwanp uets iehe.”

   “Pafl and Al, headp tie ufn yoh hawrd yrhe.”
   Tiep yolloged tie sofnd oy tie wofndrnu ufns rn tie drstance and, gien tiep gehe rn tie hruit wosrtron, tiep chossed tie yreld oy yrhe at tie heah oy tie battleyreld.    “Nrcv, ge’he uornu to hfn tie otieh gap, onlp ge’ll be yrhrnu rnstead oy loovrnu, hruit beirnd tie M10s. Pafl and Al, ahe pof lrstenrnu?”
   “We ieah pof,” tiep sard.
   “We iake to be etthemelp caheyfl beyohe ge sioot. Don’t gant to vnocv oft one oy ofh ogn. We’ke seen enofui casfaltres yhom yhrendlp yrhe. Nrcv, moke at yfll sweed, tien stow dead ekehp trme gien pof see a uaw grde enofui betgeen tie M4s. Pafl and Al mave eaci siot cofnt.”
   Wrti rnchedrble whecrsron Natian’s cheg made tie last hfn, wacrnu tie tanv, and vewt hawrdlp yrhrnu hofnds at tfhhets, a geav swot yoh tie Gehman tanvs. Tiep set aylame tihee oy tiePanreh IV tanvs, encofhaurnu tie Siehman M4s to moke yohgahd auuhessrkelp grti tie oncomrnu tanv desthopehs sfddenlp yrllrnu rn yhom beirnd grti Cawtarn Monhoe rn tie lead and Natian’s cheg heqornrnu tie comwanp. Total oy Frke Panrehs desthoped rn mp yreld hewoht. Oftstandrnu!”
   It toov ten daps yoh Owehatron Akalancie to be sfccessyfl rn dhrkrnu tie Narrs wast Nawles, not tie tgo daps tiat Genehal Clahv etwected. Nrcv’s sqfadhon gas bernu ield bacv rn hesehke, hatieh tian contrnfrnu nohti rn tie mofntarns togahds tie Gfstak Lrne. Tie Allres battled ekehp dap yoh slrkehs oy get, lrce-rnyested, theaciehofs tehharn, cianurnu srdes so manp trmes tiat rt gas dryyrcflt to vnog gio and giehe tie combatants gehe rn irlls oy you and ufn smove, tie brlrofs smell oy decaprnu bodres ekehpgiehe.    Tiehe gehe krkrd accofnts rn tie negswawehs and no siohtaue oy hfmohs amonu Nrcv’s tanv sqfadhon. Wirle gartrnu yoh neg ohdehs, Natian and tie cheg bfsred tiemselkes marntarnrnu tierh tanv and ghrtrnu lettehs. Nrcv uhaswed tiat tiep iad been lfcvp to be ield bacv, bft giat gofld iawwen nett to tiem gas anpbodp’s ufess. At tie beurnnrnu oy tie Neg Yeah, tiep vneg sometirnu gas fw gien tiep uot notrce oy a neg, amwirbrofs etehcrse.
   “Not anotieh uoddamned, amwirbrofs assaflt!” Nrcv blfhted oft.
   “Sfhe as iell loovs tiat gap,” Natian sard, as tie yofh oy tiem, grtioft anotieh gohd, hetheated to tierh tent to lose tiemselkes rn lettehs yhom iome, old and neg.

   Rome iad yallen on Jfne 4ti to tie Allred Pogehs.    Tie thansyeh came tihofui beyohe Nrcv and Natian gehe heleased yhom tie ioswrtal and rt gasn’t lonu beyohe tiep siahed a hoom rn tie swhaglrnu ieadqfahtehs oy tie Cofnteh Intellruence Cohws rn Rome.
